 From the ramparts of the Red Fort, the Prime Minister was claiming to provide electricity to the Nagla Phatela village of Hathras after 70 years of independence, but in reality there is no electricity in that village till date
 enditivi ne gaanv main jaakar pataa kiya to hakeekat saamne aa gai
 This village, about 150 km from Delhi, has electric poles installed by the central government eight months ago, electric poles have been installed on the pillars, transformers have also been installed, but unlike the claims of the Prime Minister, electricity has not reached here yet
 
 gaanv ke pradhan yogesh singh kaa kahana he ki aath maheene se bijli kaa intjaar he lekin bijli nahin ai pradhanmantri jo bole vah galat bole hai
 It is true that this village, with a population of about 3500, did not have electricity line till 8 months before independence
 lekin yahaan ke log kareeb 20 saal se gaanv ke baahar lagi sinchai kii vighut line se katiyaa daalkar lakdi ke khambhon ke jariye apano gharon tak bijli panhucha rahe hai or bijli vibhaag uskaa bill bhi bhejtaa he
 However, such connections are only in a few households

 bharat main sendha namak kaa ekmaatr strot himachal pradesh main sthiti mandi he
 Gujarat, Tamil Nadu and Rajasthan account for 96 percent of the total salt production of the country

5 million tonnes of salt produced in excess of the requirement

 yahi haal diwali ke baad vaapasi kii tikaton kaa bhi he
 Reservation in all important express trains is over
 haalat yah he ki kai trainon main vatting list kii tikaten bhi nahin mil rahi hai
 There are reports from many cities that even those who line up for tickets in the morning could not get reservation
 aarakshan kendron par logon ne der raat se hi adda jamaa liya, lekin counter khulte hi rigerveshan phul hone kii soochna milane lagi

 is baar 23 oktober ko diwali he
 After that day the return tickets ran out in a few seconds
